(Hankou) The coffin of the late Chairman Yang will be moved from Hankou to the newly built Provincial Library on Snake Mountain in Wuchang at 9:00 AM on the morning of the 2nd, and a public memorial service will be held at a later date. The funeral procession from Hankou and Wuchang has been detailed by the funeral office, and is expected to arrive at Pinghu Gate at 11:00 AM. The entire city of Wuhan will lower its flag to half-mast on the 2nd to express condolences. (1st Central News Agency Dispatch)

Page 4

The Siege of Jingyuan City Has Been Completely Lifted; The National Army Has Chased to the Banks of the Yellow River

(Lanzhou) Military news: A certain division of the National Army advanced north from Guocheng, Jingyuan to suppress the bandits. Fierce battles took place on the 29th and 30th, and another great victory was won. The troops of the division are now in Jingyuan, and the siege of the city has been completely lifted. The details are as follows: It was found that the pseudo-31st Army and the independent division of the pseudo-4th Army, which were defeated by the National Army in the Yiyuantou Baihu area in the southern district of Jingyuan, fled north under the cover of night. The National Army divided into left and right wings and pursued them at full speed. At dawn on the 29th, they encountered the bandits on the high ground west of Xizhai, Lishu'er, and Wangjia. The bandits stubbornly resisted from the dangerous terrain, and the National Army took advantage of the victory to launch a fierce attack, and has advanced to the Hongbaozi area 40 miles north of Guocheng. The corpses of bandits were scattered everywhere, and the number of casualties was no less than a thousand, especially many middle and lower-level pseudo-military officers. More than 300 people were captured, more than 200 long and short guns, more than 100 horses, and a lot of baggage were seized. The remnants of the bandits fled west to the mountains west of Hongbaozi and north to the Tongjingyuan Avenue. Near Daleizi at noon, the bandits reunited with some of the pseudo-4th and 5th Armies that had fled from both sides, and invaded the position in an attempt to resist stubbornly. The National Army arrived at the location and launched a fierce attack on the bandits, and the bandits were defeated soon. More than 100 people were captured, more than 30 horses were seized, and 50 short guns were seized. The bandits died and were injured countlessly. The remnants fled east, and the National Army divided into two groups and followed them day and night. At Shenshi on the 30th, they chased to the banks of the Yellow River near Heibaokou and Hongzuizi. It happened that some of the bandits were crossing the river, and were killed by the National Army, and those who were drowned in the river were countless, and 6 empty boats were destroyed. The two ferries and the upper and lower Baizhuzi and other places east of Qingyuan have all been recovered. The siege of Jingyuan City has been completely lifted, and the National Army is still continuing to search and suppress the bandits and advance. (1st Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Lanzhou) Zhu Mao Xu He's remnant bandits searched for civilian leather rafts and wooden boards in various areas of Jingyuan, transported them to the river bank, and crossed the river one after another. The National Army waited until the remnants on the east bank were cleared, and then crossed the river to pursue them, annihilating them all in one fell swoop, so as to prevent them from penetrating into the counties west of the river. According to people from the front, since the bandits fled to Gansu, they have been running east and west, and have been unable to gain a foothold anywhere. They lack bullets, clothing, and food, and cannot get a full meal for several days. At this time, they are still wearing single-layer clothes. The area west of the river is barren and sparsely populated. Even if the bandits fled in, they will freeze and starve to death without being chased. In recent days, the National Army's suppression has been like destroying dead trees and rotten wood. The day when they will be completely wiped out is at hand. (1st Central News Agency Dispatch)

Huang Ligui's Remnant Bandits Were Defeated and Retreated

(Fuzhou) Huang Ligui's remnant bandits recently fled to Zhengwei Township in Jianou and Dajiaozhen in Yanping, looting dozens of men and women, and extorting huge sums of money. Li Yutang's division sent a team to aggressively suppress them, capturing and killing the bandit leader Lu Shengxiang and more than a dozen bandits, and seizing one machine gun and seven rifles. The bandits were unable to resist and retreated to the nearby deep mountains. Our army is still tightly encircling and suppressing them. (1st Dispatch)

Wei Lihuang Inspects the Border Area of Three Provinces

Liuan Wei Lihuang, the director of the Henan-Hubei-Anhui Border Area, set out from Liuan by car on the 27th of last month to inspect the situation in various parts of the border area, passed through counties such as Shutong, and camped in Taihu that night. On the next day, he walked to Saxipu, which belongs to Tai. On the 30th, he made detailed inspections and condolences to the troops stationed along the way to Yingshan County, Hubei Province, and the people. He arrived in Luotian on the 31st and headed towards southern Henan. (1st Central News Agency Dispatch)

Conference on Repairing and Defending the Yellow River in Three Provinces

(Jinan) The Hebei-Shandong-Henan Yellow River Repair and Defense Association held a meeting in Jinan today and resolved many major cases, such as the Yellow River Committee allocating funds to repair and guard the Shandong Dike. (1st Dispatch)

(Jinan) At 2:00 PM on the 1st, the Yellow River Conservancy Association held a conference on repairing and defending the Yellow River in the three provinces of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan in the West Flower Hall of the Provincial Government. Han Fuqu, Kong Xiangrong, Zheng Zhaojing, Tang Qiyu, the directors of the Yellow River Affairs Bureau of the three provinces of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan, Yellow River Conservancy Association staff, and Yellow River affairs personnel attended, totaling more than 20 people. The Yellow River Conservancy Association drafted proposals including: 1. Organize the 1937 Yellow River Survey and Repair Design Team; 2. Establish a Yellow River Repair and Defense Engineering Team; 3. Build a Yellow River Dike Automobile Station to facilitate transportation; 4. Install Yellow River defense telephones in the three provinces; 5. For the 1937 repair and defense transportation, please ask the relevant state-owned routes to allocate vehicles to assist; 6. Stipulate the unified dike name of the three provinces, etc., for a total of eight items. (1st Central News Agency Dispatch)

The Ministry of Finance Explains the Ambiguity of Taxation

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance, according to Xiao En's request to interpret the ambiguity of the Provisional Regulations on Income Tax, approved that the lottery winnings from the aviation highway construction bonds belong to the income of the first category of temporary profit-making enterprises, and income tax should be levied at the tax rate stipulated in Article 4 of the Provisional Regulations on Income Tax. Lottery winnings from savings associations belong to the income of the third category of deposit interest, and income tax should be levied at the tax rate stipulated in Article 6 of the same regulations. In addition, according to the China Insurance Society's request to amend the Provisional Regulations on Income Tax to include life insurance under tax exemption, the Ministry approved that the insurance money received by life insurance policyholders, exceeding the total amount of insurance costs, is equivalent to the income of savings interest, and should be taxed according to the tax rate in Article 6 of the Provisional Regulations on Income Tax. The request to amend the regulations should not be discussed. (1st Dispatch)

Provisional Cemetery Regulations to be Promulgated and Implemented

(Nanjing) The Provisional Cemetery Regulations, having been passed by the Executive Yuan, are about to be promulgated and implemented. The regulations stipulate that each city should select a suitable location to establish a public cemetery, and each county should establish public cemeteries in its respective districts, townships, and towns. Groups, single-surname clans, or individuals may establish public cemeteries with the permission of the municipal or county government. Land for public cemeteries may be acquired by application to the ministry in accordance with the law. The height of the tomb surface above the ground shall not exceed four meters. Crematoriums may be attached to the cemetery area. Rental fees may be charged for the establishment of public cemeteries based on the tomb site and other items. Burials after the establishment of the public cemetery should be within the public cemetery. Existing private graves should be relocated to the public cemetery. Violators will be subject to fines. (A special dispatch from the 1st)

Fuzhou Business Circles Request Relief from Financial Panic; Hope Four Banks Will Accept Real Estate as Collateral, Otherwise Business Guilds Will Organize a Relief Association Themselves

Fuzhou Correspondence: The various business guilds in this city have recently observed that the decline of business in Fujian Province and the stagnation of all industries are due to the concentration of finance in the banks, which has prevented circulation in the market. Furthermore, banks do not accept credit loans or real estate mortgages, resulting in a sudden financial panic throughout the city, which has affected various counties. Before the reform of the currency system in the province, there were more than 40 money shops in the provincial capital, each issuing credit notes with an average value of more than 300,000 yuan based on their original capital and deposits. It is estimated that the total amount circulating in the market and lent to merchants was more than 12 to 13 million yuan, directly circulating in the provincial capital and indirectly flowing into various counties. Therefore, production activities and annual exports amounted to no less than 40 million yuan. As a result, although there were several political changes, they only caused temporary stagnation and were quickly restored, which was due to the activity of finance. Today, all industries are declining and production is decreasing, which is the opposite of the previous scene of killing each other in imports and exports. Although the Ministry of Finance allocated one million yuan last year to relieve the financial situation, only more than 400,000 yuan was lent out. It is really distressing that the conditions are too strict, such as a monthly interest rate of 9%, a term of 6 months, a real estate appraisal discount of half the value, and a business limited to 5,000 yuan. In addition, fire insurance and property rights registration are required, which are heavy burdens. With the short term, the interest rate must be 1.45% when combined. Large businesses cannot borrow enough with 5,000 yuan, and small businesses do not have 10,000 yuan worth of assets. The government has spent a lot of effort, but the contractors are perfunctory and the adjustments are not thorough, making it difficult to see real benefits. A meeting was specially held the other day to discuss relief measures, and it was resolved to request the government to be mindful of the fact that Fujian's commerce is on the verge of bankruptcy, and to order the four banks of China, Central, Communications, and Farmers in Fuzhou to allocate 5 million yuan specifically for the mortgage of real estate for various businesses, in order to promote commercial activities and encourage production. The interest rate is temporarily set at 4.5%, and the mortgage period is extended. If there is no overdue interest, it will be allowed to rotate for two years. The four banks of China, Central, Communications, and Farmers will each be responsible for their respective share. The four banks will each send one person to work together with the responsible person appointed by each business guild to handle the matter. The organization will be temporarily located at the Minhou County Chamber of Commerce, so that business information will not be hindered and relief will be substantial. The name of the organization and the articles of association will be drafted jointly by the responsible persons and submitted for approval after the loan is approved. If the general offices of the four banks of China, Central, Communications, and Farmers believe that this method does not comply with the regulations and cannot be accepted, then the various business guilds will have difficulty in turning around and will have to take self-rescue measures. It is proposed to allow the various business guilds to organize the Fujian Provincial Capital Financial Relief Association themselves, which will still be located at the County Chamber of Commerce, with the real estate collected by each business as a guarantee for the fund to issue Fujian Provincial Capital Commercial Mutual Aid Coupons (for example, 1 million yuan of real estate will issue 1 million yuan of mutual aid coupons, and so on, but not exceeding 3 million yuan). The association will be managed by responsible persons elected by the various business guilds who are respected, fair, and substantial. The provincial government will be requested to send personnel to supervise and audit receipts and expenditures at any time. The scope of use of the coupons will be limited to this city, and the circulation period will be set at three years, after which it will be completely terminated, so that commercial difficulties can be slightly relieved and the crisis can be resolved. The resolution has now been made into a memorandum and sent to the Chamber of Commerce for submission to the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Industry, the Fujian Provincial Party Headquarters, and the Fujian Provincial Government, requesting approval of the request and ordering the four banks of China, Central, Communications, and Farmers in Fuzhou to investigate and handle the matter.

An Analysis of Recent Chinese Finances (Middle)

— Sun Huai Ren

The historical inability of Chinese finance to balance revenue and expenditure, which is almost identical to the situation in other countries, is caused by the excessive expansion of military and debt expenditures. However, the deficits of the recent two or three years also contain a new factor, namely the reduction of tax revenue—here, the reduction of tariffs is obviously the most significant.

In the budgets of the last three years, the tax revenue for the 23rd year was 73.1 million yuan, and for the 24th year, it was 69.6 million yuan, a decrease of 3.5 million yuan compared to the previous year. In the most recent 25th year, the total tax revenue was 68 million yuan, a decrease of 1.6 million yuan compared to the previous year, and a decrease of 5.1 million yuan compared to the year before. This figure is still a grand and dignified budgetary assumption, and in reality, it may be even more drastically reduced. For example, the difference between the budgeted and finalized figures for tax revenue in the 22nd year is as shown in the final table: (Unit: Thousands of Yuan)

Here, except for the salt and consolidated taxes, all were less than the budgeted amount. In Chinese fiscal revenue, customs duties have always been the most important, but in recent years they have been declining in a straight line. According to the statistics of the 24th year's customs yearbook, customs revenue has been decreasing year by year in the last five years. In the 24th year, only 31.5 million yuan was collected, a decrease of 70 million yuan compared to the figure in the 20th year of the Republic of China. This reduction in customs duties is partly due to the reduction in imported goods in recent years, and partly due to the increasing prevalence of smuggling. According to news reports earlier this month, the loss of customs duties due to smuggling in North China alone since August of last year has reached 90 million yuan. As for the salt tax, as a result of efforts to increase the tax rate and change the weighing system (changing the Sima scale to the market scale, which is about 20% different) in recent years, it has been increasing year by year. In the 24th year of the Republic of China, the total salt tax revenue was 184 million yuan, an increase of 14 million yuan compared to the figure in the 20th year of the Republic of China five years ago. As for the consolidated tax, it is also increasing due to the increase in the tax rate and the increase in the types of goods. The revenue in the 24th year of the Republic of China was 116 million yuan, an increase of 36 million yuan compared to the 20th year of the Republic of China. Therefore, the changes in the revenue of the three major taxes, customs, salt, and consolidated tax, in the last five years are not worth the loss. The total increase in salt and consolidated taxes is only 50 million yuan, while the customs duty has decreased by 70 million yuan.

Today, the external pressure is becoming more and more serious, and customs duties may be even more reduced. As for the salt tax, it will probably not increase any more (the riots of salt farmers in the north and south and the surge of salt grabbing are all indicating that the salt tax burden has reached its maximum limit). Moreover, there is another reason why the salt tax has increased in the past, which is not that people actually consume so much salt, but that the salt farms urged to transport the salt out as much as possible, and at the same time, the tax was levied on the transported salt. Therefore, the increase in the salt tax in the past partly contained the nature of spending money in advance. Only the consolidated tax has more prospects. The central government's unification is becoming more and more complete, and of course the consolidated tax is also becoming more and more increased. But it is absolutely impossible in fact to make up for the reduction of customs duties with the increased consolidated tax! In the tax revenue example of the 22nd year that we mentioned earlier, although the actual revenue of most of the taxes was less than the budgeted amount, fortunately, because there was a large increase in the salt and consolidated taxes, the total amount of actual tax revenue still exceeded the total budgeted amount. But the situation is different now. In the most recent 25th year, customs duties will decrease no matter what (in the case where smuggling cannot be stopped, the decrease in customs duties should not be a problem. Even if the smuggling is suppressed, I am afraid that the reduction of the tax rate is already inevitable, so of course it will also reduce customs revenue); the salt tax has entered a standstill state, and it can no longer be like the 22nd year, which will increase above the budgeted figure; and the reduction of various taxes other than the consolidated tax is even more expected. Here, only the consolidated tax and the income tax are relatively close to the budget, but the total annual revenue of the two is only 13.78 million yuan.

The authorities are not unaware of this gradual downward trend in tax revenue. Therefore, the budget for tax revenue in the 25th year has been reduced by several million yuan compared to the previous two years. But although the budget for tax revenue in the 25th year has been reduced, the expenditure in the 25th year is an unprecedentedly large amount. Therefore, in order to seek the suitability of the revenue and expenditure budget on the surface, the revenue other than taxes is deliberately inflated as a matter of policy (see the previous list). For example, the net profit of state-owned businesses is mostly the surplus of the Central Bank and the interests of various official shares. Like last year, although the Central Bank obtained huge profits due to the nationalization of silver, this is temporary in the end. Without the premise of continuing to create new state-owned enterprises, it is absolutely difficult for the net profit of state-owned businesses to have such a figure every year as last year. Originally, in the draft budget for the 25th year, this net profit had been listed as 28 million yuan less than the previous year, but in order to seek the surface suitability of revenue and expenditure, it was still listed as more than 41.39 million yuan.

From the above, looking at the revenue side of the budget for the most recent 25th year, we have already discovered its three major defects. The first is the reduction of tax revenue, the second is the inflation of other revenue, and the third is the increase in debt revenue. Judging from these three points alone, it is enough to explain that recent finances are somewhat difficult to balance. Especially the increase in debt revenue not only indicates that recent finances cannot be balanced, but also implies that they are somewhat difficult to balance. Because the current increase in debt is implying that the future expenditure on debt service will be greater. Moreover, the conditions for issuing bonds in China in recent years have been very harsh. For example, from the 16th to the 22nd year of the Republic of China, a total of 113 million yuan of domestic debt was issued, but the government actually received only about 65 million yuan, which is about 57% of the face value. Such an improper issuance not only causes undue losses to most of the people, but also makes it difficult for finances to be balanced forever. In the past, more than 100 million yuan of public debt was issued, but before February of this year, the central finance still had a shortfall of 24 million to 27 million yuan per month. This is precisely to illustrate how much of a "putting the cart before the horse" measure is the public debt policy to adjust the financial imbalance.

In such extreme financial difficulties, the central government has begun a new balancing strategy, which is the forced exchange of public debt in February of this year, exchanging the 31 types of public debt issued in the past for five types of unified public debt, totaling 146 million yuan, extending the repayment period by an average of ten years. This reduces the annual expenditure on debt service and frees up some funds to issue new public debt. The main new public debt is the 340 million yuan of the Reconstruction Public Debt. The reason why the debt revenue in the budget for the 25th year is more than the previous two years is because the bond issuance fund is more settled. The Reconstruction Public Debt issued this year was originally said to be used for production undertakings and the completion of the legal tender policy, but according to news reports: "This public debt is not circulated in the market, nor is it sold publicly in the securities market. Most of it is deposited in the Central, China, and Communications banks as a guarantee to prepare for the issuance of banknotes. The central government has already overdrawn 150 million yuan from the banks in the past six months, and will need at least 150 million yuan in the next six months, totaling 300 million yuan. However, the Reconstruction Public Debt is issued at a discount of 98% of the face value, totaling about 310 million yuan, which is only enough for half a year after repaying the bank overdraft." (March 16, Beiping Morning Post) Thus it can be seen that the government does not want to give up the policy of balancing revenue and expenditure with public debt.

After the public debt consolidation in February of this year, the annual repayment of principal and interest on public debt can be reduced by about 40% compared to the figures before the consolidation in the first one or two years. The 40% fund that is reduced can at most issue another 67 million yuan of public debt. Now the Reconstruction Public Debt has been issued for more than 300 million yuan, plus the 15 million yuan of loan revenue in the budget for the 25th year (in reality, it must be more than this number). By next year, I am afraid that public debt will be difficult to issue again. Then, how will the public debt policy be used?

Current Affairs Commentary

Reading the 23rd Fiscal Year Financial Report

— Ren

Our nation's central finances, since the 18th year of the Republic, have been the subject of annual financial reports published by the Ministry of Finance. These reports aim to inform the people of the actual state of income and expenditure, serving as a basis for learning from the past and planning for the future. This intention is commendable. The situation for the 23rd year and subsequent periods has been released today, encompassing tens of thousands of words, meticulously categorized and analyzed. It details the difficult and turbulent financial situation of the past two years, along with the process of planning and reform. After reading it repeatedly, we deeply admire the authorities' ability to exert their utmost effort, summon their greatest courage, and overcome all difficulties, leading the finances towards gradual stability. Furthermore, the report's conclusion states, "What the government desires in terms of finance is not merely balancing income and expenditure, but also to make finance increasingly sound, enabling surplus resources to develop domestic economic resources and improve the people's lives." These few words are particularly pertinent. However, based on our review of the income and expenditure situation in the report, we believe that achieving this ideal state still faces obstacles and requires further efforts from the authorities. Please allow us to elaborate.

Traditionally, discussions on financial management emphasize "adjusting expenditure to match income." This principle of finance is undoubtedly true during times of peace and prosperity. However, when the nation faces difficulties and the economy declines, rigidly adhering to this principle can lead to numerous difficulties and even financial chaos. Recently, our nation's expenditures have been increasing annually, while income has not kept pace, resulting in persistent financial deficits. According to the financial report's figures, this situation was particularly pronounced in the 23rd year, with deficits reaching 20.8% of total net expenditures. However, a portion of this deficit was due to government investments, so the net shortfall was only around 13%, a decrease compared to the 22nd year. This phenomenon, in the current situation riddled with problems, may be a welcome sign. However, the ideal of balanced income and expenditure is still distant. We sincerely hope that the authorities can make further efforts in this regard, which would address the crux of China's financial problems.

How can we achieve balanced income and expenditure? The financial report outlines several principles for us, with the following three points related to finance itself: First, all unnecessary or unproductive expenditures should be reduced, with savings allocated to production and construction purposes. Second, tax officials should be selected and trained to increase administrative efficiency. Third, existing taxes should be reorganized and sound new taxes should be introduced to increase revenue without increasing the burden on the people. If these three principles can be implemented gradually over time, the resulting increase in tax revenue should make it easier to balance income and expenditure. However, this cannot be achieved overnight. While the current authorities' determination to reorganize finances is not limited to just balancing income and expenditure, we believe that seeking a balance between income and expenditure is the only essential goal for today's turbulent financial situation. Only by balancing income and expenditure can we then gradually implement other improvements, addressing urgent matters first and delaying less pressing ones, thus achieving twice the result with half the effort.

The current imbalance between income and expenditure is indeed, as the financial report states, due to a sharp decline in tax revenue. This decline is partly due to external pressures, such as rampant smuggling, and partly due to the domestic economic downturn. This decrease in income, caused by both internal and external factors, cannot be reversed through financial policies in the short term. However, in a passive sense, the pressure on finances can be reduced by using financial policies, namely by "adjusting expenditure to match income." While adjusting expenditure to match income is not the ideal financial practice, it is a means of working diligently to overcome difficulties in the current situation of internal and external challenges. Therefore, we absolutely agree with the first half of the aforementioned first principle. However, we believe that the latter half, which states, "savings should be allocated to production and construction purposes," should be limited. Only those production and construction projects that cannot be delayed should be undertaken. If they can be delayed, they should not be pursued simply because there are surplus funds, thus saving financial expenditures and reducing future financial deficits. Furthermore, to achieve the goal of adjusting expenditure to match income and balancing income and expenditure, strict adherence to the financial budget is essential. As the financial report states, "A more effective budget system must be established to control various expenditures." This is also crucial today. If the budget is not effective, how can we hope to balance income and expenditure? For example, the income and expenditure for the 23rd year each exceeded the budget for that year by 103.1 million yuan and 11.3 million yuan, respectively.

In summary, we deeply believe that the authorities can achieve their ideal of finance through their utmost efforts. However, based on our limited understanding, achieving this ideal must begin with adjusting expenditure to match income, controlling income and expenditure, and achieving balance. Then, over time, gradual reforms can be implemented to restore finance to the correct path.

Japan Plans to Facilitate Military Transport, Connecting Transportation Between Korea and Manchuria, All Korean Railways to be Managed by the South Manchuria Railway, Iron Bridges to be Built on the Tumen and Yalu Rivers

(Tokyo) A landmark policy of removing the economic "border" between Korea and Manchuria and realizing a unified Korea-Manchuria has been decided in principle after the meeting between the Governor-General of South Korea and Commander Ueda of the Kwantung Army on the Tumen River. Taking this opportunity, the issue of unifying the Korea-Manchuria Railway after entrusting the management of all national railways in Korea to the South Manchuria Railway is proceeding formally. Establishing the unification of the Korea-Manchuria transportation system is not only an important issue in economic terms but also in military terms. Therefore, from the sixth to the fourteenth year of Taisho, the South Manchuria Railway was entrusted with the construction and management of all national railways in Korea for this reason. During the Manchurian Incident, the South Manchuria Railway promised to manage 328.5 kilometers of Korean railways north of Chongjin and the two ports of Chongjin and Unggi, first realizing the unification of transportation between North Korea and "Manchukuo." Currently, Korea and Manchuria are responding to each other, and after the railways are fully connected, the "Manchukuo" government's so-called five-year plan for industrial construction, in addition to the three iron bridges currently connecting Manchuria and Korea on the Yalu and Tumen Rivers, has decided to add several more lines, making Korea-Manchuria transportation even closer. At this time, following the precedent of past years, entrusting the management of all national railways in Korea to the South Manchuria Railway and realizing the unified management of the Korea-Manchuria Railway is becoming increasingly supported by the Kwantung Army and the South Manchuria Railway. Therefore, it seems that the Korea-Manchuria authorities will begin concrete research in the future. (Alliance News Agency dispatch, 1st)

(Changchun) The Japanese and puppet authorities, seeing that the righteous army is active and emerges without warning on the Manchuria-Korea border, making "suppression" extremely difficult, have decided to implement Korea-Manchuria transportation connections. They will build a new iron bridge on the Yalu River between Andong and Shinuiju in Korea to facilitate transportation. The South Manchuria Railway Construction Bureau has been commissioned to survey the site, and construction is scheduled to begin in November of this year. The construction cost is 4 million yuan, and the project is expected to be completed within three years. Furthermore, the Korea-Manchuria border river bridge construction agreement stipulates that each party is responsible for 3 million yuan in construction funds, to be completed within seven years. The formal signing date for this agreement is reportedly scheduled for December 10 in Changchun. (China United News Agency dispatch, 1st)

US Election Campaign Ends, Differences and Similarities in the Platforms of the Two Major Parties, Roosevelt Delivers Final Speech

(Washington) As the election campaign draws to a close, the platforms put forward by the Democratic and Republican parties differ not in their goals but in their means. Regarding issues such as providing relief for the unemployed, improving society, implementing public works, curbing trusts, controlling industry and commerce, and protecting individual freedoms and rights, either one party advocates for them, or the other party supports them to a considerable extent. They are not entirely incompatible.

Republican presidential candidate Landon's criticisms of the Roosevelt administration are particularly focused on the following five points: (1) unbalanced budget; (2) after the government established commercial agreements with fourteen countries, the domestic market has been occupied by foreign goods; (3) waste of national funds due to relief for the unemployed; (4) since the implementation of the government's current agricultural policy, it has been necessary to import foreign agricultural products to meet domestic needs; (5) the New Deal, especially the National Industrial Recovery Act, violates the Constitution.

President Roosevelt replied that (A) although the amount of national debt has increased, the situation has improved and is easier to bear than in 1932, before the Democratic Party came to power; (B) since the government established commercial agreements with various countries, the total value of exported goods has increased by $680,000,000 compared to 1932; (C) relief for the unemployed is urgent, and accurate statistics are not yet available, so it is inappropriate to criticize arbitrarily; (D) the reason why the United States imports foreign agricultural products is due to the devastation of fields and crops by droughts in the past two years, but the situation of farmers has indeed improved; (E) the current Constitution should correspond to actual needs. (Havas News Agency dispatch, 31st)

(New York) President Roosevelt delivered his final election campaign speech at Madison Square Park today, strongly criticizing powerful figures in the country who are now trying to restore the best doctrine of a government that is fond of quietude and inaction. He said that this kind of force united to resist a presidential candidate is unprecedented in American history. These people are determined to make things difficult for him, and he particularly welcomes their dislike. He wants to hear people say that the selfish and power-hungry people in his first government have met their match, and he also wants to hear that in his second government, these people have surpassed their masters.

When delivering his speech today, President Roosevelt did not specify whether he would restore the National Recovery Administration and the Agricultural Adjustment Administration, but he broadly answered Republican candidate Landon's questions about the purposes of the New Deal measures, saying that its purposes were to reduce working hours, increase wages, end child labor, support collective bargaining, and promote mutually beneficial trade between countries. President Roosevelt continued, "We must continue to strive to achieve these goals because we have only just begun to build the nation." President Roosevelt also said that it is now time to continue to seek welfare for farmers. The government intends to do its best to stop the accumulation of huge surpluses in order to prevent the sharp decline in agricultural product prices. The government will also encourage farmer cooperation plans, crop insurance, and stable food supply. President Roosevelt concluded by saying, "There is war and much talk of war in the world today. We do not want to be involved in either. While protecting our own coasts, we will continue to eliminate the roots of domestic unrest and hostility, because these accidents easily make the people victims of those who seek private gain through foreign wars. All those who profit from war are not on our side in this election campaign."

The people who support President Roosevelt are mostly laborers and middle-class citizens, which seems to be inversely proportional to the fashionable Republicans who support Landon. When Roosevelt stood up and began his speech, the crowd cheered deafeningly. Roosevelt was very excited when he spoke, and the emotions of the audience were stirred. (Reuters dispatch, 31st)

St. Louis: Republican presidential candidate Landon delivered his final campaign speech here today, saying that the absurd actions of the New Deal are sufficient to prevent a true recovery. The government wants to evade responsibility and has repeatedly broken its promises, resulting in a great loss of national confidence. Landon also summarized the current problems, saying that the New Deal completely avoids answering these questions. (National News Agency dispatch, 31st)

Non-Intervention Issue: Soviet Reply; Refuting Item by Item the Accusations of Italy and Germany

(London) – Regarding the accusations by Italy and Germany that the Soviet government has violated the Spanish Civil War non-intervention agreement, the Soviet government sent out two notes on October 27 to refute them. French Foreign Minister Meets with the Ambassadors of Italy, Germany, and Belgium; Inquiring about Their Stance on the Locarno Conference; Much Deliberation on the Wording of the Italian Letter

(Paris) – Foreign Minister Delbos held important talks with the German Ambassador to France, Count Welczek, the Belgian Ambassador to France, Count Kerchove de Denterghem, and the Italian Ambassador to France, Cerruti, at the Foreign Ministry this afternoon. It is heard that what the Foreign Minister discussed with the ambassadors of Germany, Belgium, and Italy was mostly about the future of the Locarno Five-Power Conference. Earlier last month, King Leopold of Belgium issued a declaration advocating the restoration of a neutral status. Subsequently, Italian Foreign Minister Count Ciano visited Germany and held important talks with Führer Hitler. Afterward, Germany, Belgium, and Italy have decided on a new stance regarding the Locarno Conference. Therefore, Delbos specially invited the ambassadors of the three countries to inquire about it. In addition, the Spanish issue was also mentioned. Delbos also discussed the drafting of the letter of credence of the newly appointed French Ambassador to Italy, Saint-Quentin, with Italian Ambassador Cerruti. Italy requires that when the newly appointed French ambassador goes to Rome to take office, the letter of credence should state "His Majesty, King of Italy and Emperor of Abyssinia, Emmanuel." France believes that this title inevitably implies recognition of Italy's annexation of Abyssinia. Therefore, this issue is still under discussion. (Havas dispatch, 31st)

Lindbergh's Transatlantic Flight; Tenth Anniversary Next Year; French Aviation Department Decides to Hold; New York-Paris Air Race

(Paris) – The famous American aviator Major Lindbergh flew solo across the Atlantic Ocean from America to Paris in 1927. Next year marks the tenth anniversary of this event. The French Aviation Department has decided to hold a New York-to-Paris air race to commemorate Major Lindbergh's great achievement. Aviation Minister Guito recently made a statement to a reporter from the Hardliner News on this matter, saying, "In order to encourage domestic and foreign individuals to participate in this competition, the government has decided to establish four prizes: a first prize of 1.5 million francs, a second prize of 1 million francs, a third prize of 500,000 francs, and a fourth prize of 300,000 francs. France plans to form at least three teams to participate in the competition. The first team will be composed of the famous aviators Rossi and Codos (who departed from New York on August 7, 1933, flew across the Atlantic Ocean and traversed the European continent, reaching Rayak, Syria, covering 9,104.7 kilometers, setting a world record for direct-distance flight). The second team plans to have General Poumège fly a plane on behalf of the French Air Force to participate in the competition. As for the third team, the French airline will select the best pilot, mechanic, and radio operator to form it. Generally speaking, the famous aviator Mermoz (who has made multiple flights on the Paris-South American Brazil route) will be chosen as the pilot. As for the preparation of the competition and the matching of aircraft engines, the task should be entrusted to experts in long-distance flight, such as the famous aviator Costes (Costes once flew directly from Paris to Qiqihar and also flew across the Atlantic Ocean from east to west)." (Havas dispatch, 31st)

Situation in North China Suddenly Turns Tense; Kwantung and North China Army Headquarters Have New Decisions; Will Stir Up Trouble Using the Taiyuan and Zhong Company Incident

Tianjin Correspondent – The situation in North China has suddenly shifted from calm to tense after a staff officer, Kazuchi, from the Tianjin-based Japanese Garrison Army Headquarters went to Changchun on the 28th of this month to meet with the Chief of Staff of the Kwantung Army, Itagaki, to exchange opinions. On the Suiyuan front, more than 500 troops from the puppet army of Li Shouxin were discovered on the 28th attacking the vicinity of Doufuyiaozi in Qingyi Township, northeast of Xinghe County. After a fierce battle of half a day, our army reinforcements repelled the puppet troops. However, the two bandit gangs of Wang Ying and Jin Jiasan are still lurking near Shangdu. The situation is not optimistic. Zhao Chengshou, seeing the urgency of the border situation, rushed back to Jining from Datong on the evening of the 29th and went to the forward defense on the 30th for inspection. Although it is difficult to predict when the bandit army will attack, the outbreak of war is imminent.

The defense of Suiyuan is mainly managed by Fu Zuoyi, which is quite promising. A certain party is also slightly wary and has recently been devising a strategy. They feel that they should cut off the connection between Jin and Sui and contain the Jin army from reinforcing the north. Therefore, they are considering taking action in Taiyuan, so that the Jin authorities have no time to look north and allow them to do as they please in eastern Suiyuan. This plan has now been obtained, namely, the sudden outbreak of the Taiyuan Japanese and Zhong Company incident on the 26th of this month. The Japanese Army Headquarters declared that it would engage in self-defense and resolutely punish. The cause of the incident is that a Japanese resident, Tanaka Yoshitaro, and a Japanese without a passport, Takeda Sueo, established a smuggling trading company and engaged in drug trafficking called the Hezhong Company at No. 1 Shandong Alley, Taiyuanfang, Taiyuan City. The Public Security Bureau's crackdown was ineffective. In late September, the Xieshan Hospital, next door to the company, relocated. The hospital director, Wang Junde, without the landlord's permission, transferred the site to Tanaka for the expansion of the company. The landlord did not agree and filed a lawsuit with the Shanxi District Court. The lawsuit was won and the landlord took back the house. However, Tanaka refused to leave and filed a complaint with the head of the Taiyuan Special Service Agency, Kawano, and the secretary of the consular branch, Nishi, and the chief of the police branch, Uetsuma. Kawano then protested to the Jin Sui Office. As of October 26, the matter had not been resolved. The citizens were indignant when they learned of this and were about to express their displeasure. The Taiyuan Public Security Bureau, fearing accidents, allocated more than ten soldiers to guard the Hezhong Company and the vacant Xieshan houses and sent Tanaka's accomplice Takeda to Zhengzhou. Kawano said that this was anti-Japanese and insulted overseas Chinese, and reported it to Tianjin. The Japanese Army Headquarters held a special meeting on the evening of the 28th. On the afternoon of the 29th, Kazuchi visited Consul General Horiuchi stationed in Tianjin to discuss opinions. Horiuchi was trying to expand the police power in North China and wanted to set up a deputy consulate and a police station in Taiyuan, but had repeatedly negotiated with the Jin authorities without results. He took this opportunity to discuss with Kazuchi. In addition to the Japanese Army Headquarters sending a telegram to Kawano to file a serious protest with the Jin Sui Office, the consulate sent four patrolmen on the 30th, led by Section Chief Sekikawa and Police Inspector Ura, and several police branch officers and officials, planning to expand the police station in the name of protecting overseas Chinese after arriving in Taiyuan. The Japanese Army Headquarters, in order to achieve its goals, deliberately released the air that the lives of overseas Chinese in Taiyuan were in danger, and was a latent threat for expanding the scope. In fact, there are a total of thirty-four Japanese and Korean people in Taiyuan. They all moved to Takahashi's residence on the 28th. The Jin authorities are doing their best to protect them, and the public has no anti-Japanese facts. Life and property are as safe as ever, which is not as bad as the Japanese side is spreading. Their intentions are far-reaching and have other purposes. Although our protection is thorough, it is difficult to prevent the expansion of the issue itself. (30th)

Large-Scale Japanese Military Exercise; Regiment Against Regiment War; Taking Beiping as a Hypothetical Target of Attack; Encounter Battle and Night Battle on the 30th; Gunfire Raged and Emotions Were Extremely Tense

Beiping Correspondent - The autumn exercises of the Japanese garrison in North China, which have been underway since the 26th, were completed on the 28th after individual regimental exercises. There was a one-day rest on the 29th. On the 30th, three days of regimental-against-regimental exercises continued, with the 1st Regiment stationed in Ping and the 2nd Regiment stationed in Tianjin and Tong as the main force. More than 400 soldiers, artillery, and others from the infantry of the 1st Regiment stationed in Ping carried 7 large and small tanks, 20 heavy trucks loaded with military supplies, and 4 motorcycles, departing from the Japanese barracks in Dongjiaominxiang at 5:30 a.m. on the 30th, passing through Qianmen, out of Yongdingmen, crossing the southern suburbs, and heading towards Anding. Another 400 or more infantry soldiers and 30 or more cavalry soldiers from the Japanese army stationed in Ping also left the barracks on foot at the same time, carrying more than ten large carts loaded with food, passing through You'anmen, crossing the southern suburbs, and also going to Anding. Together with more than 800 Japanese soldiers from the 1st Regiment stationed in Fengtai, there were about 1,700 people, gathering near Sihezhuang and Zhangzhuangchang. At the same time, more than 1,000 Japanese soldiers from the 2nd Regiment stationed in Tianjin and Tongxian also departed from Langfang and Tongxian around 6:00 a.m. on the 30th and arrived at Longjiafang and Hejiafen on the Tongxian border to gather. At 9:00 a.m., the two regiments mobilized at the same time for counter-exercises. At about 10:00 a.m., they encountered each other in the Dahungcun and Majuqiao area, fighting an encounter battle. For a time, gunfire raged and emotions were extremely tense, taking Beiping as a hypothetical target of attack. The two sides tried their best to attack and resist, and stalemate until 5:00 p.m. The Japanese troops from Tianjin and Tongxian finally retreated eastward, and the Japanese troops from Pingfeng also followed them forward, and then ended, camping and having dinner in Mazhuang and Saoziying. Starting at 9:00 p.m., they continued the night battle until 12:00 p.m. On the morning of the 31st, they continued counter-exercises in the northeastern area of Saoziying and camped overnight in Xiaogaozhuang and Sujiafen. On November 1st, they continued counter-exercises in the same place. During these three days, the counter-exercises of the Japanese 1st and 2nd Regiments were led by Regiment Commanders Mutaguchi and Kayashima, and conducted under the command of Brigade Commander Kawabe. The regimental counter-exercises ended on the evening of the 1st, and Beiping was assumed to have been occupied by the attacking army. On the 2nd, they all gathered in Tongxian. At that time, Japanese Commander-in-Chief Tashiro went to Tongxian from Tianjin to inspect and direct the Japanese army to conduct exercises from Tongxian to Beiping. Early on the morning of the 3rd, it was planned to have 600 Japanese soldiers enter Chaoyangmen, pass through Ping City, exit Fuchengmen, and go straight to the western suburbs for exercises. This action also meant that Beiping had been occupied by the attacking army. Chief of Staff of the Japanese Army Headquarters Qiaoben Qun arrived in Ping from Tianjin on the afternoon of the 30th and went to Tongxian to arrange everything. On the 3rd, there was a large-scale exercise in the western suburbs all day long, with the division headquarters participating, involving about 7,000 people. On the morning of the 4th, it was inspected by Tashiro at Babaoshan and related personnel were invited to visit. When the Japanese army held large-scale exercises in the western suburbs, our army stationed in Xiyuan will also organize a team to visit. During the period of large-scale exercises by the Japanese army, the people showed a lot of anxiety. Those who are nervous have already purchased grain and stored rice to prepare for unexpected events. (30th)

Illegal Merchants Transporting Grain Out of the Province; Hebei Province Citizens Fear a Food Shortage; Flour and Rice Prices Soaring Rapidly; Certain Factions Extensively Purchasing Rice to Supply Military Provisions

Baoding Correspondence: Each county in Hebei Province fortunately had a bumper harvest this year. The people were celebrating the ample food supply, and expecting grain prices to fall. However, contrary to expectations, the prices of flour and rice have soared relentlessly. The public food supply issue has triggered immense panic. The reasons for this are summarized below:

Public Food Supply Panic

An investigation into the food supply in Hebei Province reveals that, apart from flour, which has traditionally relied on shipments from Shanghai merchants, other grains are mostly supplied by the various counties. However, the source of these grains has almost been cut off in recent times. When available for sale, market prices are about one and a half times higher than in the past. Green-label flour from the Qianyi Company in this province, which used to sell for only three yuan and five jiao, has now risen to four yuan and five jiao. Other red, blue, and yellow-label flours have also increased by seven or eight jiao each. As for Shanghai flour, it has risen to five yuan and is still unavailable. Rice costs sixteen yuan per bag, while locally-produced Fuji rice is also fourteen yuan and five jiao. The highest-grade Saigon rice has surged to around nineteen yuan per bag. Even the lowest grade of high-grade Min Dang rice cannot be purchased for less than fourteen yuan. Other grains such as sorghum, mung beans, and wheat have each risen by two or three jiao. The general populace is filled with worry, leading to widespread panic. The weather has turned severely cold recently, which has a critical impact on social order. Although farmers in the countryside have had a bountiful autumn harvest themselves, much of their produce was bought up by rice and flour merchants at low prices early on. Now they can only watch as they lose out on substantial profits. Moreover, they still have to buy back grain at higher prices, suffering losses and lamenting their helplessness.

Reasons for Price Increases

This province was originally the most developed agricultural area. This year's bumper harvest should have prevented a food supply panic, however: (1) Major farmers, seeing the instability of the times, are buying and storing rice and flour, and refusing to sell their own grain. (2) Small farmers rely solely on their annual grain production to purchase clothing and supplies. They sell off most of their harvested grain, causing them to feel the pinch of food shortage. (3) Flour companies and major grain merchants bought up most of the agricultural produce at low prices before the autumn harvest. (4) Unscrupulous merchants are taking the opportunity to manipulate market prices. (5) Certain factions have sent people to various places to purchase large quantities of grain and rice to supply military provisions. (6) Illegal merchants are transporting grain out of the province on a large scale. All of these factors have caused a great panic over the food supply in this province. The lower and middle classes, in particular, are feeling insecure. (October 31)

Grand Celebration of the Yellow River's Calm Waters in Hebei, Shandong, and Henan Provinces; Kong Xiangrong Leads River Workers in Sacrificing to Yu the Great; A Three-Province River Defense Conference Continues After the Celebration

Jinan Correspondence: The Yellow River flows through nine provinces and has historically been a source of disasters. Breaches and overflows have occurred frequently, causing particularly severe damage. Since Kong Xiangrong, the Chairman of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, has been in charge of affairs, he has successfully closed breaches three times at Fenglou, Guantai, and Dongzhuang. This year, the Yellow River's water level rose, with a flow rate exceeding 17,000 cubic meters per second, a record-breaking volume. Through Kong's efforts, together with all the personnel of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, the chairmen of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan provinces, and the heads of the river affairs bureaus, as well as tireless round-the-clock efforts by the workers, the situation was turned from danger to safety, averting breaches. This is truly a great fortune for the country and its people. To commemorate the Yellow River's calm waters and encourage future efforts, the Yellow River Conservancy Commission and the authorities of the three provinces jointly initiated the Grand Celebration of the Yellow River's Calm Waters in Hebei, Shandong, and Henan Provinces, held in Jinan. At the same time, a three-province river construction and defense conference was convened to determine Yellow River construction and defense measures, with the aim of preparing in advance and ensuring lasting calm. Due to the significant importance of the conference, representatives from various regions arrived in Jinan to participate and offer congratulations. The commemorative gifts sent were dazzling. At 8:00 AM, Kong Xiangrong and Wang Kairu, the Director of the Shandong River Affairs Bureau, along with personnel from the Yellow River Conservancy Commission and the River Affairs Bureau, went to the Great King Temple on the banks of the Luokou River to offer sacrifices to Yu the Great and past sages who had governed the river. At 12:00 noon, the Calm Waters Celebration was held at the Jinde Assembly Hall. Participants included Han Fuqu, the Chairman of Shandong Provincial Government; Ge Guangting, the Chairman of the Jiaoji Railway Commission; Jiang Kanghu, a Doctor of Sociology; Zheng Zhaojing, the representative of the Economic Commission; Qin Fen, the Secretary-General representing Tang Qiyu; Du Yuliu, the representative of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council and the Director of the Hebei River Affairs Bureau; Wang Liren, the representative of the Henan Provincial Government and the Director of the Henan River Affairs Bureau; Zhu Guangcai, the Secretary-General's representative; Liu Xiaoying, the representative of the National Economic Commission's Water Conservancy Association; Liang Chaoyu, the representative of the North China Water Conservancy Commission; Wang Kairu, the Director of the Shandong River Affairs Bureau; as well as various Shandong division commanders, regiment commanders, provincial party committee members, heads of various agencies, representatives of various organizations, representatives of people from various counties, and personnel from the Yellow River Conservancy Commission and the Shandong River Affairs Bureau, totaling no less than a thousand people. Hundreds of plaques, couplets, silver shields, and silver tripods were displayed. After the meeting, photos were taken, meals were shared, and theatrical performances were held. Each attendee was given a commemorative medal. At 6:00 PM, Han Fuqu and Kong Xiangrong hosted a banquet for the representatives at the Jinde Assembly Hall, with enthusiastic atmosphere and a grand occasion. It is said that next year's Calm Waters Celebration will be held in Hebei, and the year after that in Henan. Today (31st), after the Calm Waters Celebration concludes, the three-province river defense conference will continue tomorrow (2nd).

Japanese Police Plan to Establish a Branch in Baoding; Police Officer Men Guan Sent to Baoding to Survey Locations; Future Plans Also Include Establishing One in Cangzhou

Baoding Correspondence: Baoding is the most important town south of Beiping on the Pinghan Railway Line. Anhui Local Bank Establishes a Southeast Financial Network; Direct Remittances with Zhejiang, Jiangsu, Jiangxi, and Fujian; Exchange and Circulation of Subsidiary Coinage

Wuhu Correspondence: The construction and development of resources in the southeastern transportation provinces have progressed rapidly in recent years. Villages on the brink of collapse due to emptiness are gradually reviving. Business in various towns and cities is also becoming more prosperous. However, many construction plans still need to be continued. Therefore, the need for economic support is also very urgent. In view of this, Anhui Provincial Local Bank, in order to mutually promote economic ties with neighboring provinces and promote economic construction, has initiated the establishment of a financial network for the southeastern provinces. Starting with Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Fujian, and Anhui provinces. Once the initial stage has been successful, the scope will be expanded. Anhui Provincial Local Bank has separately agreed with the local banks of the above four provinces on financial liaison measures to implement mutual remittances and the exchange and circulation of subsidiary coinage in each province. The procedures are not only simple, but the remittance fees are also low. All banks are committed to serving local interests and mutually promoting the full economic development of each province. Today, Anhui and Zhejiang provinces are the first to start remittances. Anhui includes the Wuhu Head Office, Anqing, Bengbu, Tunxi Branch Offices, and 34 county offices. The remittance locations in Zhejiang Province include (Head Office) Hangzhou, (Branch Offices) Shanghai, Jiaxing, Huzhou, Ningbo, Shaoxing, Haimen, Lanxi, Wenzhou, (Offices) Haining, Yuhang, Xiaoshan, Jiashan, Pinghu, Tongxiang, Changxing, Nanxun, Shuanglin, Xinshi, Sian, Fenghua, Zhenhai, Shengxian, Shangyu, Huangyan, Cixi, Yuyao, Jinhua, Ninghai, Linhai, Quzhou, Longyou, Ruian, Lishui, Zhuji, Jiande, Chongde, Shipu, Wenling, Aojiang, and other places. Remittances with Jiangsu, Fujian, and Jiangxi provinces will be implemented as soon as agreements are signed. In addition, economic relations will be established with Guangdong Province to facilitate the transportation and sale of products. Because the provincial government is planning to mutually exchange Anhui rice and Guangdong sugar in order to consume domestic products. If the banks of the two provinces are successfully connected, the exchange method may be realized as soon as possible. In addition, the 120+ provincial and county agricultural warehouses established by the provincial government for the storage, pledging, transportation, and sale of rice and grain are under vigorous construction, and nearly 40% are now complete. In addition to Quanjiao and Langxi counties, which have already loaned out more than 60,000 yuan, the agricultural warehouses in Wuhu, Xuancheng, Dangtu, and Chaoxian counties, which have the largest capacity, will soon be lent out separately, and will handle the storage, pledging, transportation, and sale of rice and grain. Near Qingdao, the Yisheng Steamer Collides with a Sailboat; Total Losses Estimated at Around 6,000 Yuan; Negotiations for Compensation are Currently Underway

Qingdao Correspondence: Zhang Tingqin, a resident of Huangdao, runs a shipping business. He owns a sailboat, thirteen feet in length, and employs Liu Zengli from Xuejiadao as a sailor. They travel back and forth between Qingdao and Haixi. On the morning of the 30th, at around 9:00 AM, they were carrying twelve passengers and their luggage when they sailed from Huangdao to this port. Due to the excessive waves at sea, the sailboat's rudder malfunctioned. They originally sailed from Huangdao to Xiaogang, but were blocked by the wind. The boat changed direction and sailed straight towards the west side of the wireless radio station on Tuandao. At that time, the Yisheng steamer of Jardine Matheson & Co., which had come from Shanghai to Qingdao, had rounded Tuandao and was sailing along the sea route to the Dagang Wharf. Because the steamer was traveling very fast, it met the sailboat on the west side of the radio station. Unable to avoid a collision in time, the two boats collided, and the sailboat was completely destroyed. The cabin immediately filled with water, and the fourteen passengers and sailors fell into the sea. Cries for help were heard everywhere. Seeing that an accident had occurred, the crew of the Yisheng steamer immediately lowered a lifeboat and rescued the passengers to safety. The destroyed sailboat was towed to Dagang and docked at the first wharf. However, all the goods and money and luggage carried by the passengers had been washed away by the water. The total loss is estimated at more than 6,000 yuan. The passengers and the owner of the boat, together with the person in charge of the Yisheng steamer (an Englishman), went to the maritime affairs section of the port authority to request handling of the matter. Li Shiyi and others, who were elected as representatives by the passengers, are responsible for negotiating with the Yisheng steamer for compensation for the losses.

Songjiang; Four Suspects Apprehended in Sijing

Patrol officers from the Fifth Police Substation in Sijing apprehended four suspects of a certain kind, named Shi Guoyuan, Fa Jing, Xu Wenjing, and Hong Jingshui, on the night of the 31st. They were jointly escorted to the county bureau on the 1st for interrogation and further investigation.

Kunshan; Banning the Production of Bamboo Chip Tokens

Shops in remote towns in this county often have capital shortages and poor turnover, so they privately produce bamboo chip tokens for circulation among the people, disrupting the financial order. The county government has obtained approval to issue a ban. It has been learned that the Xintai Fish Shop in Jinjiazhuang in the Fifth District is also producing bamboo chip tokens, divided into 500-wen and 1,000-wen denominations. After being discovered by the county government, the Public Security Bureau has been ordered to investigate and deal with the matter, and to recover and destroy the tokens within a specified period.

Wuxi; Organizing a Waterborne Baojia System

Zhang Da, the Director of the Public Security Bureau in this county, in addition to actively handling the establishment of police administrative districts, has also taken note of the fact that there are numerous rivers and streams in this county, and waterborne theft cases occur from time to time. The original water patrol team has limited police force, and patrols and arrests are often inadequate. Therefore, he has ordered the various branch bureaus to transfer 20 police cadets to the control of Song Tao Wei, the captain of the water patrol team, who is responsible for organizing a waterborne baojia system. In addition, four police stations will be established in important ports, and detective squads will be added to specifically investigate and arrest waterborne thieves in order to maintain security.

Standardizing Weights and Measures

Since the new weights and measures system in this county has been promoted by the county government, Qin Hemen, the inspector, has been conducting inspections of various industries and shops in the urban area. This has now been completed. Merchants and the people can faithfully implement the new system. However, the situation in the rural areas is not consistent, so it is necessary to actively promote and earnestly inspect. Qin has decided to proceed to the various districts and towns from November 16th to continue the work, so that business practices will not be inconsistent, and the new system can be standardized. The county government has separately ordered the various districts and public security bureaus to assist in the implementation in advance. In addition, all old instruments used in the rice, bean, and miscellaneous grain industries will be abolished and replaced with the new system.

Changshu; Murder of a Child in Zhenmen Temple

A child murder case occurred yesterday at the Zhenmen Temple in Meili in the Second District. The murderous mother has been arrested and sent to the county government for investigation and handling. Xue Er, a resident of Xuejiajiao in that area, was a laborer in a cloth factory. Last year, he became unemployed and unable to make a living, so he resorted to theft. His mother, Ms. Xu, repeatedly taught him, but to no avail. The day before yesterday, Xue went to the home of Tang Pei, a tax collector, to steal, but was caught. Tang hated him and sent him to his mother, instructing her to kill him. Ms. Xu was temporarily deceived by Tang and tied up her son with a rope and beat him to death on the spot with a wooden hammer. His head was broken, his brains burst, and the scene was extremely tragic. The matter was reported to the township head, who reported it to the county for investigation. An official was dispatched on the 31st to verify that the incident was true and arrested the murderous mother, Ms. Xu, to await trial in the county.

Yangzhou; Epidemics are Prevalent in Jiangbei

The weather in Jiangbei this year, from spring to autumn, has been abnormal, resulting in particularly numerous epidemics, such as black fever, malignant malaria, and diphtheria. In addition, since entering autumn, it has not rained for two months, so winter wheat and barley cannot be planted. People feel very uneasy. Coupled with frequent fires and a lack of drinking water, the autumn sun has been very strong for days. It is rumored that locusts are very active in the Huaibei area. It is rare to see locusts in late autumn like this. The future is really worrying.

Gaoyou; More Than Ten Passenger Boats Robbed by Bandits

More than ten passenger boats moored in the river east of Hanliuzhuang in the Donghui Town of the Second District of this county were coveted by bandits. Before dawn on the 29th, more than 20 bandits suddenly arrived, armed with guns, and searched and robbed the boats separately. Fortunately, the residents of the village and farmers from nearby villages learned of the bandit alarm and fired guns to demonstrate, and the bandits, fearing trouble, hurriedly fled with the loot. The losses were not great.

Rice Mills are Purchasing Rice from Other Ports

The price of rice in this county is more than five yuan per shih. In view of the minimal profits, rice merchants are going to Wuhu, Changzhou, and other places to purchase rice. It is said that it is several jiao cheaper per shih than in this county. Although the shipping costs are higher, the profits are also substantial.

Hangzhou; Silkworm Cocoon Loan of 600,000 Yuan

The Zhejiang Provincial Silkworm Silk Control Committee, in order to improve the silkworm cocoon baking equipment of cocooneries in various counties, has conducted a loan of 600,000 yuan for cocoon baking to the China Farmer's Bank and the Zhejiang Local Bank. After several discussions, the two banks have agreed, and a draft contract has also been drawn up. The two banks will each bear 300,000 yuan, with a monthly interest rate of 9%, to be repaid within the year from 1937. The collateral is the operating income and all property of the cocooneries receiving the loans, and the Silkworm Silk Control Committee will provide a second guarantee. The formal contract will be signed with the banks before the cocooneries bake the silkworm cocoons, and interest will accrue from that day.

Huzhou; Police Arrest a Opium Offender

The Nanjie Police Station of the city's Public Security Bureau received a report at 3:00 PM on the 30th that Yu Maotou, at No. 41 Xiaohetou, was smoking opium. Upon receiving the report, police chief Qiu Zitian dispatched police officers who found the opium paraphernalia and arrested Yu Maotou and transferred him to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Ningbo; Ming Dynasty Cannon Unearthed for Coastal Defense

Xinpu Yan, in Yuyao, is located on the coast and was the site where General Qi Jiguang of the Ming Dynasty stationed troops to suppress Japanese pirates. It is rumored that there was a cannon submerged in the river there (now the north end of the Xinpu Temple). Gu Yian, the captain of the Xinpu Yan Guard Team, believing that the river was dry at this time and excavation would be easier than usual, ordered all the team members to dig in the river on the 28th. After a while, the cannon was indeed found. The surrounding people came to watch. The cannon's bore was more than one foot in diameter, and although it had been submerged for a long time, it was still awe-inspiring. It has now been transported to the team headquarters and will be cleaned and mounted in a nearby strategic location for observation.

Haizhou; Appealing for Postponement of House Tax

The First Branch of the Guanyun County Public Security Bureau recently obeyed orders to investigate the shops and residential houses of merchants and residents in order to provide a basis for future collection of house tax. The merchants and residents of shops and residential houses throughout the city are worried about increased burdens and have collectively appealed to the County Chamber of Commerce, various township offices, and various industry associations to request a postponement of the tax. The chamber and associations believe that the coastal areas suffered from floods last year, and agricultural land was submerged. The planting season was missed, and the wheat harvest this year was meager. Moreover, the dredging of the river lasted for half a year, and the people's strength was exhausted. The people's livelihoods in the entire county are on the verge of bankruptcy. It goes without saying that the urban residents are especially reliant on the salt industry for their livelihood. This year, not only was the spring salt harvest lost, but transportation and sales have also stagnated, making life difficult. House prices have fallen. On the surface, the residents' houses look magnificent, but in reality they cannot afford to eat or wear clothes. If the house tax is implemented again, where will the people be placed? Under these special circumstances, we can only ask the government to give the people a chance to recuperate and wait for the social situation to improve before implementing the house tax. This seems to be considerate of both the situation and the law. Therefore, the County Chamber of Commerce, the various township offices, and the various industry associations have jointly telegraphed the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance and the county government and other relevant agencies, requesting approval to temporarily postpone the collection of taxes in order to alleviate the people's difficulties.

Cherry Tree Blossoms in Autumn

Cherry trees bloom in March and April. Now it is autumn, and the leaves have fallen, and the branches have withered. However, a cherry tree planted in the backyard of the First District Office in Guanyun County recently sprouted leaves first, and then bloomed flowers, which are as brilliant as in spring.

The match between Tung Wah and Portugal was held yesterday at Recreation Ground, with hundreds of spectators. As a result, Tung Wah won 6-0, with three goals in each half, surpassing the 4-1 victory in the previous friendly match. Referee He Chunhui was unable to attend due to circumstances, and the league temporarily found a replacement. The lineups for both sides are as follows:

Tung Wah

Cheung Wing Choi

Li Ning Li Yee Chen

Wan Cheung Wah Suen Shun Tai Lun King Hui Man Kwai Ka Yau Leung

Collins

Gonsalves Weekes

Roliz Sheffield Soares

First Half: Yesterday morning, there was light rain. Recreation Ground was still able to proceed as usual due to the better field conditions. However, when the two teams lined up, drizzle was still falling. As a result of the coin toss, Tung Wah attacked first. After a few rounds, the Portuguese team launched a large-scale attack, but fortunately, the defense was extremely solid, and there was no need to worry about crossing the line. Although Tung Wah had several good opportunities, they ultimately failed due to the lack of coordination in the front line. Iron-legged Suen Kam Shun was also unable to display his strengths, while the Rocha brothers and Andrade of the Portuguese side frequently appeared in Tung Wah's territory, causing waves of shock in the defense. The intensity of the Portuguese attack and the frequent missed opportunities by Tung Wah made the audience feel dim. After about thirty minutes of stalemate, both sides still maintained their virgin status. Until Fung Wan Yau obtained the ball from the center line and made a high pass to the enemy's territory, Wan Cheung Wah passed to the center line, Ka Yau Leung hooked backwards, and Hui Man Kwai broke through, finally breaking the stalemate. Once the record was opened, luck also followed. One minute later, Suen Kam Shun dribbled into the area, and the Portuguese defender, in desperation, pulled him down, resulting in a penalty. Koo Sheung Yeung executed it and scored successfully (2-0). Shortly after, Cheung Wah launched another attack from the periphery, forcing a corner kick. Suen Kam Shun took the kick, which landed right in front of the goal. Collins jumped to catch it but missed, and Ka, Hui, and Tai rushed in, with Yau Leung tapping it in. The first half ended with a score of 3-0.

Second Half: The second half began, and Tung Wah's attack became more intense. They missed two good opportunities. Five minutes into the half, Ka Yau Leung pointed with his whip, and Tai Lun King headed the ball in, opening the record again. Not long after, Ka had another excellent opportunity, sprinting to the baseline and hooking the ball in, but unfortunately, there was no one to receive it, and Collins caught it, which was a great pity. After several rounds, Tung Wah's army directly approached the enemy's territory again. Hui and Tai broke through the crowd and drove straight in. At the penalty line, Tai Lun King rushed out and shot, hitting the target with precision. After this, the Portuguese attack became strong again, with Rocha and Lopes shooting twice, both of which were extremely dangerous. On Tung Wah's side, Suen Kam Shun hit the post and the ball bounced out, Tai Lun King's fierce shot was forced into a corner kick, and Ka Yau Leung was also trapped by the Portuguese defenders. Good opportunities were missed again and again. Both sides attacked and defended, holding each other for about twenty minutes. In front of the Portuguese goal, it became Tung Wah's artillery position, with concentrated firepower and accurate range. Collins managed to catch them one by one, saving them from danger. After a short pause, Tung Wah's penalty area also became chaotic, but they did not fall. Time flew by quickly, with only one minute left before the end of the match. Suen Kam Shun, who had been feeling frustrated for a long time, got a ball, rushed out alone, and shot from twenty yards, flying straight into the net. Collins was caught off guard and helpless. Before the center line kick, the whistle had already sounded for a long time. Tung Wah won 6-0 against Portugal.
